CUDA Kernel Files (`.cu`) in `_ext-src/src/`\n\n### `/app/pointnet2_ops_lib/pointnet2_ops/_ext-src/src/ball_query_gpu.cu` (54 lines)\nImplements **ball query** -- finding points within a given radius for each query point.\n- **`query_ball_point_kernel`**: For each batch and query point, iterates over all input points, collecting indices of neighbors within the squared radius. If a new point is found within range, it is recorded. The first neighbor found \"fills\" all nsample slots with that index (deterministic fallback).\n- **`query_ball_point_kernel_wrapper`**: Host-side launcher using `opt_n_threads(m)` block size and the current CUDA stream.\n\n### `/app/pointnet2_ops_lib/pointnet2_ops/_ext-src/src/sampling_gpu.cu` (229 lines)\nImplements two operations:\n1. **Gather/Scatter** (`gather_points_kernel` / `gather_points_grad_kernel`): Forward gathers features at given indices; backward uses `atomicAdd` to scatter gradients back.\n2. **Furthest Point Sampling (FPS)** (`furthest_point_sampling_kernel`): An iterative algorithm that repeatedly selects the point farthest from the currently selected set. Uses a parallel reduction (shared memory `dists`/`dists_i` arrays) with a template-based block size switch (512, 256, 128, ..., 1) to handle various device capabilities. Maintains a `temp` array tracking the minimum distance from each point to the set of already-sampled points.\n\n### `/app/pointnet2_ops_lib/pointnet2_ops/_ext-src/src/interpolate_gpu.cu` (154 lines)\nImplements three operations:\n1. **3-Nearest Neighbors** (`three_nn_kernel`): For each query point, finds its 3 nearest neighbors in a reference set by maintaining `best1/best2/best3` running minimums.\n2. **3-Interpolate (forward)** (`three_interpolate_kernel`): Weighted sum of features at the 3 nearest neighbor locations.\n3. **3-Interpolate (backward)** (`three_interpolate_grad_kernel`): Uses `atomicAdd` to distribute gradients back to the original features proportionally to the interpolation weights.\n\n### `/app/pointnet2_ops_lib/pointnet2_ops/_ext-src/src/group_points_gpu.cu` (75 lines)\nImplements:\n1. **Group Points (forward)** (`group_points_kernel`): Gathers features for each grouping operation, using the `opt_block_config(npoints, c)` for 2D thread grid.\n2. **Group Points (backward)** (`group_points_grad_kernel`): Scatters gradients back via `atomicAdd`.\n\n---\n\n## 3. Build Configuration (`setup.py`)\n\n**File:** `/app/pointnet2_ops_lib/setup.py` (39 lines)\n\n- Uses `setuptools` with `torch.utils.cpp_extension.CUDAExtension`\n- Automatically discovers all `.cpp` and `.cu` source files and all header files under `_ext-src/src/` and `_ext-src/include/`\n- Sets `TORCH_CUDA_ARCH_LIST` to support architectures: 3.7+PTX, 5.0, 6.0, 6.1, 6.2, 7.0, 7.5\n- Compiles with `-O3` for both host (cxx) and device (nvcc) code\n- NVCC also gets `-Xfatbin -compress-all` for smaller binary size\n- The extension module is named `pointnet2_ops._ext`\n- Requires `torch>=1.4`\n\n---\n\n## 6. Key components:\n- **JIT fallback**: If the pre-compiled `_ext` module cannot be imported, it JIT-compiles the CUDA/C++ sources at runtime using `torch.utils.cpp_extension.load`.\n- **Autograd Functions** (wrapping the C++ `_ext` ops):\n  - `FurthestPointSampling` -- FPS on point clouds\n  - `GatherOperation` -- gather features at indices (with backward)\n  - `ThreeNN` -- find 3 nearest neighbors\n  - `ThreeInterpolate` -- weighted interpolation of features (with backward)\n  - `GroupingOperation` -- group features by index (with backward)\n  - `BallQuery` -- ball query neighbor search\n- **nn.Module wrappers**:\n  - `QueryAndGroup` -- combines ball query + grouping, optionally appending xyz delta features\n  - `GroupAll` -- groups all points (radius = entire cloud)\n\n### `/app/pointnet2_ops_lib/pointnet2_ops/pointnet2_modules.py` (209 lines)\n**High-level PointNet2 building blocks**:\n- `build_shared_mlp()` -- constructs 1x1 Conv2d MLP stacks with optional BatchNorm\n- `_PointnetSAModuleBase` -- base class for Set Abstraction Modules; combines FPS + grouping + MLP + max pooling\n- `PointnetSAModuleMSG` -- multi-scale groupings (multiple radii/samples/MLPs)\n- `PointnetSAModule` -- single-scale version of the above\n- `PointnetFPModule` -- feature propagation module that interpolates features from a coarser level to a finer level using 3-NN inverse-distance weighting\n\n### `/app/pointnet2_ops_lib/MANIFEST.in` (1 line)\n`graft pointnet2_ops/_ext-src` -- ensures the C++/CUDA source tree is included in source distributions.\n\n---\n\n## Architecture Summary\n\nThe library implements the core geometric operations from the **PointNet++** paper (Qi et al., 2017).
